Auditing the cache DB

from fastlite import Database
from pathlib import Path
import pandas as pd
import json
from evaluatr.frameworks import IOMEvalData
from evaluatr.mappr import (format_enabler_theme, format_crosscutting_theme, 
                            format_gcm_theme, format_srf_output, find_srf_output_by_id)
traces_dir = Path.home() / '.evaluatr' / 'traces'
db_path = traces_dir / 'pipeline_cache.db'
db = Database(db_path)
print("Tables:", db.t)
Tables: sections_cache, theme_tagging_cache
sections = db.t.sections_cache
themes = db.t.theme_tagging_cache

for d in sections():
    print(report_names[d['report_id']])
    sections_list = json.loads(d['sections_selected'])
    for section in sections_list:
        print(f"- {section}")

# Delete all rows?
# for row in sections(): sections.delete(row.report_id)
def delete_themes():
    for row in themes(): 
        themes.delete((row['report_id'], row['stage'], row['framework'], row['framework_category'], row['framework_theme_id']))

def get_core_themes(report_id): 
    df = pd.DataFrame(list(themes()))
    return df[(df['report_id'] == report_id) & (df['is_core'] == 1)]

# Load framework data
eval_data = IOMEvalData()
import re 

def clean_markdown_for_excel(text):
    """Remove markdown formatting but keep structure with newlines"""
    # Remove markdown headings but keep the text
    text = re.sub(r'^#+\s*', '', text, flags=re.MULTILINE)
    # Remove bold/italic markers
    text = re.sub(r'\*\*([^*]+)\*\*', r'\1', text)
    text = re.sub(r'\*([^*]+)\*', r'\1', text)
    # Keep newlines for structure
    return text.strip()

def get_theme_description(row):
    """Get formatted theme description as seen by LLM"""
    framework = row['framework']
    category = row['framework_category']
    theme_id = row['framework_theme_id']
    
    try:
        if framework == 'SRF' and category == 'Enablers':
            theme = next(t for t in eval_data.srf_enablers if t.id == theme_id)
            formatted = format_enabler_theme(theme)
        
        elif framework == 'SRF' and category == 'Crosscutting Priorities':
            theme = next(t for t in eval_data.srf_crosscutting_priorities if t.id == theme_id)
            formatted = format_crosscutting_theme(theme)
        
        elif framework == 'GCM':
            theme = next(t for t in eval_data.gcm_objectives_small if t['id'] == theme_id)
            formatted = format_gcm_theme(theme)
        
        elif framework == 'SRF' and category == 'Outputs':
            output_context = find_srf_output_by_id(eval_data, theme_id)
            if output_context:
                formatted = format_srf_output(output_context)
        
        # Clean markdown and truncate
        cleaned = clean_markdown_for_excel(formatted)
        return cleaned
        # return cleaned[:1000] + "..." if len(cleaned) > 1000 else cleaned
    except:
        return "N/A"
    
    return "N/A"
df['theme_description'] = df.apply(get_theme_description, axis=1)

import openpyxl
from openpyxl.styles import Alignment

# Select and reorder columns
columns_order = ['report_id', 'report_name', 'stage', 'framework', 
                 'framework_category', 'framework_theme_id', 'theme_description', 
                 'is_core', 'reasoning', 'open_codes', 'your_tag']
df_export = df[columns_order]

# Create output directory
output_dir = Path('tagging_review')
output_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)

# Export each report to separate Excel file
for report_name in df_export['report_name'].unique():
    if pd.isna(report_name):
        continue
    
    report_df = df_export[df_export['report_name'] == report_name]
    output_file = output_dir / f'{report_name}_tagging.xlsx'
    
    # Write to Excel
    report_df.to_excel(output_file, index=False, engine='openpyxl')
    
    # Format cells to wrap text
    wb = openpyxl.load_workbook(output_file)
    ws = wb.active
    
    # Set column widths first
    ws.column_dimensions['A'].width = 35  # report_id
    ws.column_dimensions['B'].width = 30  # report_name
    ws.column_dimensions['C'].width = 10  # stage
    ws.column_dimensions['D'].width = 12  # framework
    ws.column_dimensions['E'].width = 12  # framework_category
    ws.column_dimensions['F'].width = 25  # framework_theme_id
    ws.column_dimensions['G'].width = 60  # theme_description
    ws.column_dimensions['H'].width = 10  # is_core
    ws.column_dimensions['I'].width = 60  # reasoning
    ws.column_dimensions['J'].width = 50  # open_codes
    ws.column_dimensions['K'].width = 10  # your_tag
    
    for row in ws.iter_rows():
        for cell in row:
            cell.alignment = Alignment(wrap_text=True, vertical='top')
    
    wb.save(output_file)
    print(f"Exported: {output_file}")
